\subsection{Detailed Description}
Controlling media parameters. 

{\bfseries Multicast}

Call using rtp multicast addresses are supported for both audio and video with some limitations. Limitations are, no stun, no ice, no encryption.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Incoming call with multicast address are automatically accepted. The called party switches in a media receive only mode.
\item Outgoing call willing to send media to a multicast address can activate multicast using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+multicast()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_gab1fdd4ac8c4ba4e09b665d3959a1b850} or \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+audio\+\_\+multicast()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga6d4f13f9667c595bee9d2d0e4177ec7d}. The calling party switches in a media listen send only mode. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\item If enabled, outgoing calls put a multicast address from \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+video\+\_\+multicast\+\_\+addr}{p.}{group__media__parameters_gaf3edab80f222a53c636cb3da27182712} into audio cline. In case of outgoing call audio stream is sent to this multicast address. ~\newline
 For incoming calls behavior is unchanged.

\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+rate\+\_\+control (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable adaptive rate control. 

Adaptive rate control consists in using R\+T\+CP feedback provided information to dynamically control the output bitrate of the audio and video encoders, so that we can adapt to the network conditions and available bandwidth. Control of the audio encoder is done in case of audio-\/only call, and control of the video encoder is done for audio \& video calls. Adaptive rate control feature is enabled by default. \mbox{\label{group__media__parameters_gaf54c428ef4f44158be0204ba60031627}} 
\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+audio\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+jittcomp@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+audio\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+jittcomp}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+audio\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+jittcomp@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+audio\+\_\+adaptive\+\_\+jittcomp}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}

If enabled, outgoing calls put a multicast address from \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+video\+\_\+multicast\+\_\+addr}{p.}{group__media__parameters_gaf3edab80f222a53c636cb3da27182712} into audio cline. In case of outgoing call audio stream is sent to this multicast address. For incoming calls behavior is unchanged.

{\em core} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} \\

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+echo\+\_\+cancellation()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+echo\+\_\+cancellation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables or disable echo cancellation. 

Value is saved and used for subsequent calls. This actually controls software echo cancellation. If hardware echo cancellation is available, it will be always used and activated for calls, regardless of the value passed to this function. When hardware echo cancellation is available, the software one is of course not activated. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em val} & A boolean value telling whether echo cancellation is to be enabled or disabled. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{vcap\+\_\+enabled,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{display\+\_\+enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables video globally. 

This function does not have any effect during calls. It just indicates Linphone\+Core to initiate future calls with video or not. The two boolean parameters indicate in which direction video is enabled. Setting both to false disables video entirely.

\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video\+\_\+source\+\_\+reuse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{enable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable or disable video source reuse when switching from preview to actual video call. 

This source reuse is useful when you always display the preview, even before calls are initiated. By keeping the video source for the transition to a real video call, you will smooth out the source close/reopen cycle.

This function does not have any effect durfing calls. It just indicates the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} to initiate future calls with video source reuse or not. Also, at the end of a video call, the source will be closed whatsoever for now. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em enable} & T\+R\+UE to enable video source reuse. F\+A\+L\+SE to disable it for subsequent calls. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED Ortp\+Payload\+Type$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+find\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{type,  }\item[{int}]{rate,  }\item[{int}]{channels }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get payload type from mime type and clock rate. 

This function searches in audio and video codecs for the given payload type name and clockrate.

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+audio\+\_\+codecs()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED const bctbx\+\_\+list\+\_\+t$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+audio\+\_\+codecs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the list of available audio codecs. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & The Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A list of Ortp\+Payload\+Type objects.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This list is unmodifiable. The -\/$>$data field of the bctbx\+\_\+list\+\_\+t points a Payload\+Type structure holding the codec information. It is possible to make copy of the list with bctbx\+\_\+list\+\_\+copy() in order to modify it (such as the order of codecs).

\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+nortp\+\_\+timeout (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the value of the no-\/rtp timeout. 

When no R\+TP or R\+T\+CP packets have been received for a while Linphone\+Core will consider the call is broken (remote end crashed or disconnected from the network), and thus will terminate the call. The no-\/rtp timeout is the duration above which the call is considered broken. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The value of the no-\/rtp timeout in seconds 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__media__parameters_gad27880bb917fbf5fcc8e839699ff8aa9}} 
\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Payload\+Type}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{type,  }\item[{int}]{rate,  }\item[{int}]{channels }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get payload type from mime type and clock rate. 

This function searches in audio and video codecs for the given payload type name and clockrate. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a} object \\
\hline
{\em type} & payload mime type (I.\+E S\+P\+E\+EX, P\+C\+MU, V\+P8) \\
\hline
{\em rate} & can be \doxyref{L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+Y\+L\+O\+A\+D\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+R\+A\+TE}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga2306371063fd39f746ee4db99596e8c3} \\
\hline
{\em channels} & number of channels, can be \doxyref{L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+Y\+L\+O\+A\+D\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+LS}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga5ae9e6b3f73ab7889082772130fc8467} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns N\+U\+LL if not found. If a \doxyref{Linphone\+Payload\+Type}{p.}{group__media__parameters_gaf12c1654abbcb5cffe74841fc282b7d7} is returned, it must be released with \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+payload\+\_\+type\+\_\+unref()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_gad3bd129d9e849012155b2ead58a128dc} after using it. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The returned payload type is allocated as a floating reference i.\+e. the reference counter is initialized to 0. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

0 The list is taken by the Linphone\+Core thus the application should not free it. This list is made of struct Payload\+Type describing the codec parameters.

Setting Linphone\+A\+V\+P\+F\+Default is equivalent to Linphone\+A\+V\+P\+F\+Disabled. This setting can be overriden per Linphone\+Proxy\+Config with \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+proxy\+\_\+config\+\_\+set\+\_\+avpf\+\_\+mode()}{p.}{group__proxies_ga3bbd52c26bdbc7df7fb84f804101a6d8}. {\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+device\+\_\+rotation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{int}]{rotation }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Tells the core the device current orientation. 

This can be used by capture filters on mobile devices to select between portrait/landscape mode and to produce properly oriented images. The exact meaning of the value in rotation if left to each device specific implementations. I\+OS supported values are 0 for U\+I\+Interface\+Orientation\+Portrait and 270 for U\+I\+Interface\+Orientation\+Landscape\+Right.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+native\+\_\+video\+\_\+window\+\_\+id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the native video window id where the video is to be displayed. 

For Mac\+OS, Linux, Windows\+: if not set or L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+U\+TO the core will create its own window, unless the special id L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE is given. \mbox{\label{group__media__parameters_ga33fb51a80b47473722d1c7efa2bf3102}} 
\index{Media parameters@{Media parameters}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params}!Media parameters@{Media parameters}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+network\+\_\+simulator\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{const Ortp\+Network\+Simulator\+Params $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the network simulator parameters. 

Liblinphone has the capabability of simulating the effects of a network (latency, lost packets, jitter, max bandwidth). Please refer to the o\+R\+TP documentation for the meaning of the parameters of the Ortp\+Network\+Simulator\+Params structure. This function has effect for future calls, but not for currently running calls, though this behavior may be changed in future versions. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Due to design of network simulation in o\+R\+TP, simulation is applied independently for audio and video stream. This means for example that a bandwidth limit of 250kbit/s will have no effect on an audio stream running at 40kbit/s while a videostream targetting 400kbit/s will be highly affected. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & the Linphone\+Core \\
\hline
{\em params} & the parameters used for the network simulation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__media__parameters_ga29058f8f0f1aa0f214507c55c4f50cfe}}

Set the preferred frame rate for video. 

Based on the available bandwidth constraints and network conditions, the video encoder remains free to lower the framerate. There is no warranty that the preferred frame rate be the actual framerate. used during a call. Default value is 0, which means \char`\"{}use encoder\textquotesingle{}s default fps value\char`\"{}.

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+preview\+\_\+video\+\_\+definition()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+preview\+\_\+video\+\_\+definition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Video\+Definition} $\ast$}]{vdef }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the video definition for the captured (preview) video. 

This method is for advanced usage where a video capture must be set independently of the definition of the stream actually sent through the call. This allows for example to have the preview window in High Definition even if due to bandwidth constraint the sent video definition is small. Using this feature increases the C\+PU consumption, since a rescaling will be done internally.

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em vdef} & Linphone\+Video\+Definition object \\

Sets the video size for the captured (preview) video. 

This method is for advanced usage where a video capture must be set independently of the size of the stream actually sent through the call. This allows for example to have the preview window with HD resolution even if due to bandwidth constraint the sent video size is small. Using this feature increases the C\+PU consumption, since a rescaling will be done internally.

{\em lc} & the linphone core \\
\hline
{\em vsize} & the video resolution choosed for capuring and previewing. It can be (0,0) to not request any specific preview size and let the core optimize the processing. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
